135→\t\t}\n   136→\t\tif _, err := debver.NewVersion(version); err != nil {\n   137→\t\t\tl.log.Warnf(\"kernel running version is invalid. skip kernel vulnerability detection. actual kernel version: %s, err: %s\", version, err)\n   138→\t\t\tversion = \"\"\n   139→\t\t}\n   140→\t}\n   141→\treturn\n   142→}\n   143→\n   144→func (l *base) allContainers() (containers []config.Container, err error) {\n   145→\tswitch l.ServerInfo.ContainerType {\n   146→\tcase \"\", \"docker\":\n   147→\t\tstdout, err := l.dockerPs(\"-a --format '{{.ID}} {{.Names}} {{.Image}}'\")\n   148→\t\tif err != nil {\n   149→\t\t\treturn containers, err\n   150→\t\t}\n   151→\t\treturn l.parseDockerPs(stdout)\n   152→\tcase \"lxd\":\n   153→\t\tstdout, err := l.lxdPs(\"-c n\")\n   154→\t\tif err != nil {\n   155→\t\t\treturn containers, err\n   156→\t\t}\n   157→\t\treturn l.parseLxdPs(stdout)\n   158→\tcase \"lxc\":\n   159→\t\tstdout, err := l.lxcPs(\"-1\")\n   160→\t\tif err != nil {\n   161→\t\t\treturn containers, err\n   162→\t\t}\n   163→\t\treturn l.parseLxcPs(stdout)\n   164→\tdefault:\n   165→\t\treturn containers, xerrors.Errorf(\n   166→\t\t\t\"Not supported yet: %s\", l.ServerInfo.ContainerType)\n   167→\t}\n   168→}\n   169→\n   170→func (l *base) runningContainers() (containers []config.Container, err error) {\n   171→\tswitch l.ServerInfo.ContainerType {\n   172→\tcase \"\", \"docker\":\n   173→\t\tstdout, err := l.dockerPs(\"--format '{{.ID}} {{.Names}} {{.Image}}'\")\n   174→\t\tif err != nil {\n   175→\t\t\treturn containers, err\n   176→\t\t}\n 198→\tcase \"\", \"docker\":\n   199→\t\tstdout, err := l.dockerPs(\"--filter 'status=exited' --format '{{.ID}} {{.Names}} {{.Image}}'\")\n   200→\t\tif err != nil {\n   201→\t\t\treturn containers, 207→\t\t\treturn containers, err\n   208→\t\t}\n   209→\t\treturn l.parseLxdPs(stdout)\n   210→\tcase \"lxc\":\n   211→\t\tstdout, err := l.lxcPs(\"-1 --stopped\")\n   212→\t\tif err != nil {\n l.ServerInfo.ContainerType)\n   219→\t}\n   220→}\n   221→\n   222→func (l *base) dockerPs(option string) (string, error) {\n   223→\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"docker ps %s\", option)\n   224→\tr := 246→\treturn r.Stdout, nil\n   247→}\n   248→\n   249→func (l *base) parseDockerPs(stdout string) (containers []config.Container, err error) {\n   250→\tlines := strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\")\n   251→\tfor _, line := range lines {\n   252→\t\tfields := strings.Fields(line)\n   253→\t\tif len(fields) == 0 {\n   254→\t\t\tbreak\n   255→\t\t}\n   256→\t\tif len(fields) != 3 {\n   257→\t\t\treturn containers, xerrors.Errorf(\"Unknown format: %s\", line)\n   258→\t\t}\n   259→\t\tcontainers = append(containers, config.Container{\n   260→\t\t\tContainerID: fields[0],\n   261→\t\t\tName:        fields[1],\n   262→\t\t\tImage:       fields[2],\n   263→\t\t})\n   264→\t}\n   265→\treturn\n   266→}\n   267→\n   268→func (l *base) parseLxdPs(stdout string) (containers []config.Container, err error) {\n   269→\tlines := strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\")\n   270→\tfor i, line := range lines[3:] {\n   271→\t\tif i%2 == 1 {\n   272→\t\t\tcontinue\n   273→\t\t}\n   274→\t\tfields := strings.Fields(strings.Replace(line, \"|\", \" \", -1))\n   275→\t\tif len(fields) == 0 {\n   276→\t\t\tbreak\n   277→\t\t}\n   278→\t\tif len(fields) != 1 {\n   279→\t\t\treturn containers, xerrors.Errorf(\"Unknown format: %s\", line)\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\t\tcontainers = append(containers, config.Container{\n   282→\t\t\tContainerID: fields[0],\n   283→\t\t\tName:        fields[0],\n   284→\t\t})\n   285→\t}\n   286→\treturn\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→func (l *base) parseLxcPs(stdout string) (containers []config.Container, err error) {\n   290→\tlines := strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\")\n   291→\tfor _, line := range lines {\n   292→\t\tfields := strings.Fields(line)\n   293→\t\tif len(fields) == 0 {\n   294→\t\t\tbreak\n   295→\t\t}\n   296→\t\tcontainers = append(containers, config.Container{\n   297→\t\t\tContainerID: fields[0],\n   298→\t\t\tName:        fields[0],\n   299→\t\t})\n   300→\t}\n   301→\treturn\n   302→}\n   303→\n   304→// ip executes ip command and returns IP addresses\n   305→func (l *base) ip() ([]string, []string, error) {\n   306→\t// e.g.\n   307→\t// 2: eth0: <BROADCAST,MULTICAST,UP,LOWER_UP> mtu 1500 qdisc pfifo_fast state UP qlen 1000\\    link/ether 52:54:00:2a:86:4c brd ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff\n   308→\t// 2: eth0    inet 10.0.2.15/24 brd 10.0.2.255 scope global eth0\n   309→\t// 2: eth0    inet6 fe80::5054:ff:fe2a:864c/64 scope link \\       valid_lft forever preferred_lft forever\n   310→\tr := l.exec(\"/sbin/ip -o addr\", noSudo)\n   311→\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   312→\t\treturn nil, nil, xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to detect IP address: %v\", r)\n   313→\t}\n   314→\tipv4Addrs, ipv6Addrs := l.parseIP(r.Stdout)\n   315→\treturn ipv4Addrs, ipv6Addrs, nil\n   316→}\n   317→\n   318→// parseIP parses the results of ip command\n   319→func (l *base) parseIP(stdout string) (ipv4Addrs []string, ipv6Addrs []string) {\n   320→\tlines := strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\")\n   321→\tfor _, line := range lines {\n   322→\t\tfields := strings.Fields(line)\n   323→\t\tif len(fields) < 4 {\n   324→\t\t\tcontinue\n   325→\t\t}\n   326→\t\tip, _, err := net.ParseCIDR(fields[3])\n   327→\t\tif err != nil {\n   328→\t\t\tcontinue\n   329→\t\t}\n   330→\t\tif !ip.IsGlobalUnicast() {\n   331→\t\t\tcontinue\n   332→\t\t}\n   333→\t\tif ipv4 := ip.To4(); ipv4 != nil {\n   334→\t\t\tipv4Addrs = append(ipv4Addrs, ipv4.String())\n   335→\t\t} else {\n   336→\t\t\tipv6Addrs = append(ipv6Addrs, ip.String())\n   337→\t\t}\n   338→\t}\n   339→\treturn\n   340→}\n   341→\n   342→func (l *base) detectPlatform() {\n   343→\tif l.getServerInfo().Mode.IsOffline() {\n   344→\t\tl.setPlatform(models.Platform{Name: \"unknown\"})\n   345→\t\treturn\n   346→\t}\n   347→\tok, instanceID, err := l.detectRunningOnAws()\n   348→\tif err != nil {\n   349→\t\tl.setPlatform(models.Platform{Name: \"other\"})\n   350→\t\treturn\n   351→\t}\n   352→\tif ok {\n   353→\t\tl.setPlatform(models.Platform{\n   354→\t\t\tName:       \"aws\",\n   355→\t\t\tInstanceID: instanceID,\n   356→\t\t})\n   357→\t\treturn\n   358→\t}\n   359→\n   360→\t//TODO Azure, GCP...\n   361→\tl.setPlatform(models.Platform{Name: \"other\"})\n   362→\treturn\n   363→}\n   364→\n   365→var dsFingerPrintPrefix = \"AgentStatus.agentCertHash: \"\n   366→\n   367→func (l *base) detectDeepSecurity() (string, error) {\n   368→\t// only work root user\n   369→\tif l.getServerInfo().Mode.IsFastRoot() {\n   370→\t\tif r := l.exec(\"test -f /opt/ds_agent/dsa_query\", sudo); r.isSuccess() {\n   371→\t\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(`/opt/ds_agent/dsa_query -c \"GetAgentStatus\" | grep %q`, dsFingerPrintPrefix)\n   372→\t\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, sudo)\n   373→\t\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n   374→\t\t\t\tline := strings.TrimSpace(r.Stdout)\n   375→\t\t\t\treturn line[len(dsFingerPrintPrefix):], nil\n   376→\t\t\t}\n   377→\t\t\tl.warns = append(l.warns, xerrors.New(\"Fail to retrieve deepsecurity fingerprint\"))\n   378→\t\t}\n   379→\t}\n   380→\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to detect deepsecurity %s\", l.ServerInfo.ServerName)\n   381→}\n   382→\n   383→func (l *base) detectIPS() {\n   384→\tips := map[string]string{}\n   385→\tfingerprint, err := l.detectDeepSecurity()\n   386→\tif err != nil {\n   387→\t\treturn\n   388→\t}\n   389→\tips[constant.DeepSecurity] = fingerprint\n   390→\tl.ServerInfo.IPSIdentifiers = ips\n   391→}\n   392→\n   393→func (l *base) detectRunningOnAws() (ok bool, instanceID string, err error) {\n   394→\tif r := l.exec(\"type curl\", noSudo); r.isSuccess() {\n   395→\t\tcmd := \"curl --max-time 1 --noproxy 169.254.169.254 http://169.254.169.254/latest/meta-data/instance-id\"\n   396→\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, noSudo)\n   397→\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n   398→\t\t\tid := strings.TrimSpace(r.Stdout)\n   399→\t\t\tif !l.isAwsInstanceID(id) {\n   400→\t\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n   401→\t\t\t}\n   402→\t\t\treturn true, id, nil\n   403→\t\t}\n   404→\n   405→\t\tswitch r.ExitStatus {\n   406→\t\tcase 28, 7:\n   407→\t\t\t// Not running on AWS\n   408→\t\t\t//  7   Failed to connect to host.\n   409→\t\t\t// 28  operation timeout.\n   410→\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n   411→\t\t}\n   412→\t}\n   413→\n   414→\tif r := l.exec(\"type wget\", noSudo); r.isSuccess() {\n   415→\t\tcmd := \"wget --tries=3 --timeout=1 --no-proxy -q -O - http://169.254.169.254/latest/meta-data/instance-id\"\n   416→\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, noSudo)\n   417→\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n   418→\t\t\tid := strings.TrimSpace(r.Stdout)\n   419→\t\t\tif !l.isAwsInstanceID(id) {\n   420→\t\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n   421→\t\t\t}\n   422→\t\t\treturn true, id, nil\n   423→\t\t}\n   424→\n   425→\t\tswitch r.ExitStatus {\n   426→\t\tcase 4, 8:\n   427→\t\t\t// Not running on AWS\n   428→\t\t\t// 4   Network failure\n   429→\t\t\t// 8   Server issued an error response.\n   430→\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n   431→\t\t}\n   432→\t}\n   433→\treturn false, \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\n   434→\t\t\"Failed to curl or wget to AWS instance metadata on %s. container: %s\",\n   435→\t\tl.ServerInfo.ServerName, l.ServerInfo.Container.Name)\n   436→}\n   437→\n   438→// http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSEC2/latest/UserGuide/resource-ids.html\n   439→var awsInstanceIDPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`^i-[0-9a-f]+$`)\n   440→\n   441→func (l *base) isAwsInstanceID(str string) bool {\n   442→\treturn awsInstanceIDPattern.MatchString(str)\n   443→}\n   444→\n   445→func (l *base) convertToModel() models.ScanResult {\n   446→\tctype := l.ServerInfo.ContainerType\n   447→\tif l.ServerInfo.Container.ContainerID != \"\" && ctype == \"\" {\n   448→\t\tctype = \"docker\"\n   449→\t}\n   450→\tcontainer := models.Container{\n   451→\t\tContainerID: l.ServerInfo.Container.ContainerID,\n   452→\t\tName:        l.ServerInfo.Container.Name,\n   453→\t\tImage:       l.ServerInfo.Container.Image,\n   454→\t\tType:        ctype,\n   455→\t}\n   456→\n   457→\terrs, warns := []string{}, []string{}\n   458→\tfor _, e := range l.errs {\n   459→\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Sprintf(\"%+v\", e))\n   460→\t}\n   461→\tfor _, w := range l.warns {\n   462→\t\twarns = append(warns, fmt.Sprintf(\"%+v\", w))\n   463→\t}\n   464→\n   465→\tscannedVia := scannedViaRemote\n   466→\tif isLocalExec(l.ServerInfo.Port, l.ServerInfo.Host) {\n   467→\t\tscannedVia = scannedViaLocal\n   468→\t} else if l.ServerInfo.Type == constant.ServerTypePseudo {\n   469→\t\tscannedVia = scannedViaPseudo\n   470→\t}\n   471→\n   472→\treturn models.ScanResult{\n   473→\t\tJSONVersion:       models.JSONVersion,\n   474→\t\tServerName:        l.ServerInfo.ServerName,\n   475→\t\tScannedAt:         time.Now(),\n   476→\t\tScanMode:          l.ServerInfo.Mode.String(),\n   477→\t\tFamily:            l.Distro.Family,\n   478→\t\tRelease:           l.Distro.Release,\n   479→\t\tContainer:         container,\n   480→\t\tPlatform:          l.Platform,\n   481→\t\tIPv4Addrs:         l.ServerInfo.IPv4Addrs,\n   482→\t\tIPv6Addrs:         l.ServerInfo.IPv6Addrs,\n   483→\t\tIPSIdentifiers:    l.ServerInfo.IPSIdentifiers,\n   484→\t\tScannedCves:       l.VulnInfos,\n   485→\t\tScannedVia:        scannedVia,\n   486→\t\tRunningKernel:     l.Kernel,\n   487→\t\tPackages:          l.Packages,\n   488→\t\tSrcPackages:       l.SrcPackages,\n   489→\t\tEnabledDnfModules: l.EnabledDnfModules,\n   490→\t\tWordPressPackages: l.WordPress,\n   491→\t\tLibraryScanners:   l.LibraryScanners,\n   492→\t\tOptional:          l.ServerInfo.Optional,\n   493→\t\tErrors:            errs,\n   494→\t\tWarnings:          warns,\n   495→\t}\n   496→}\n   497→\n   498→func (l *base) setErrs(errs []error) {\n   499→\tl.errs = errs\n   500→}\n   501→\n   502→func (l *base) getErrs() []error {\n   503→\treturn l.errs\n   504→}\n   505→\n   506→func (l *base) setLogger(logger logging.Logger) {\n   507→\tl.log = logger\n   508→}\n   509→\n   510→const (\n   511→\tsystemd  = \"systemd\"\n   512→\tupstart  = \"upstart\"\n   513→\tsysVinit = \"init\"\n   514→)\n   515→\n   516→// https://unix.stackexchange.com/questions/196166/how-to-find-out-if-a-system-uses-sysv-upstart-or-systemd-initsystem\n   517→func (l *base) detectInitSystem() (string, error) {\n   518→\tvar f func(string) (string, error)\n   519→\tf = func(cmd string) (string, error) {\n   520→\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, sudo)\n   521→\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   522→\t\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to stat %s: %s\", cmd, r)\n   523→\t\t}\n   524→\t\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(strings.NewReader(r.Stdout))\n   525→\t\tscanner.Scan()\n   526→\t\tline := strings.TrimSpace(scanner.Text())\n   527→\t\tif strings.Contains(line, \"systemd\") {\n   528→\t\t\treturn systemd, nil\n   529→\t\t} else if strings.Contains(line, \"upstart\") {\n   530→\t\t\treturn upstart, nil\n   531→\t\t} else if strings.Contains(line, \"File: ‘/proc/1/exe’ -> ‘/sbin/init’\") ||\n   532→\t\t\tstrings.Contains(line, \"File: `/proc/1/exe' -> `/sbin/init'\") {\n   533→\t\t\treturn f(\"stat /sbin/init\")\n   534→\t\t} else if line == \"File: ‘/sbin/init’\" ||\n   535→\t\t\tline == \"File: `/sbin/init'\" {\n   536→\t\t\tr := l.exec(\"/sbin/init --version\", noSudo)\n   537→\t\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n   538→\t\t\t\tif strings.Contains(r.Stdout, \"upstart\") {\n   539→\t\t\t\t\treturn upstart, nil\n   540→\t\t\t\t}\n   541→\t\t\t}\n   542→\t\t\treturn sysVinit, nil\n   543→\t\t}\n   544→\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to detect a init system: %s\", line)\n   545→\t}\n   546→\treturn f(\"stat /proc/1/exe\")\n   547→}\n   548→\n   549→func (l *base) detectServiceName(pid string) (string, error) {\n   550→\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"systemctl status --quiet --no-pager %s\", pid)\n   551→\tr := l.exec(cmd, noSudo)\n   552→\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   553→\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to stat %s: %s\", cmd, r)\n   554→\t}\n   555→\treturn l.parseSystemctlStatus(r.Stdout), nil\n   556→}\n   557→\n   558→func (l *base) parseSystemctlStatus(stdout string) string {\n   559→\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(strings.NewReader(stdout))\n   560→\tscanner.Scan()\n   561→\tline := scanner.Text()\n   562→\tss := strings.Fields(line)\n   563→\tif len(ss) < 2 || strings.HasPrefix(line, \"Failed to get unit for PID\") {\n   564→\t\treturn \"\"\n   565→\t}\n   566→\treturn ss[1]\n   567→}\n   568→\n   569→// LibFile : library file content\n   570→type LibFile struct {\n   571→\tContents []byte\n   572→\tFilemode os.FileMode\n   573→}\n   574→\n   575→func (l *base) scanLibraries() (err error) {\n   576→\tif len(l.LibraryScanners) != 0 {\n   577→\t\treturn nil\n   578→\t}\n   579→\n   580→\t// library scan for servers need lockfiles\n   581→\tif len(l.ServerInfo.Lockfiles) == 0 && !l.ServerInfo.FindLock {\n   582→\t\treturn nil\n   583→\t}\n   584→\n   585→\tl.log.Info(\"Scanning Lockfile...\")\n   586→\n   587→\tlibFilemap := map[string]LibFile{}\n   588→\tdetectFiles := l.ServerInfo.Lockfiles\n   589→\n   590→\t// auto detect lockfile\n   591→\tif l.ServerInfo.FindLock {\n   592→\t\tfindopt := \"\"\n   593→\t\tfor filename := range models.LibraryMap {\n   594→\t\t\tfindopt += fmt.Sprintf(\"-name %q -o \", filename)\n   595→\t\t}\n   596→\n   597→\t\t// delete last \"-o \"\n   598→\t\t// find / -type f -and \\( -name \"package-lock.json\" -o -name \"yarn.lock\" ... \\) 2>&1 | grep -v \"find: \"\n   599→\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(`find / -type f -and \\( ` + findopt[:len(findopt)-3] + ` \\) 2>&1 | grep -v \"find: \"`)\n   600→\t\tr := exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n   601→\t\tif r.ExitStatus != 0 && r.ExitStatus != 1 {\n   602→\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to find lock files\")\n   603→\t\t}\n   604→\t\tdetectFiles = append(detectFiles, strings.Split(r.Stdout, \"\\n\")...)\n   605→\t}\n   606→\n   607→\tfor _, path := range detectFiles {\n   608→\t\tif path == \"\" {\n   609→\t\t\tcontinue\n   610→\t\t}\n   611→\n   612→\t\tif path, err = filepath.Abs(path); err != nil {\n   613→\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to abs the lockfile. err: %w, filepath: %s\", err, path)\n   614→\t\t}\n   615→\n   616→\t\t// skip already exist\n   617→\t\tif _, ok := libFilemap[path]; ok {\n   618→\t\t\tcontinue\n   619→\t\t}\n   620→\n   621→\t\tvar f LibFile\n   622→\t\tswitch l.Distro.Family {\n   623→\t\tcase constant.ServerTypePseudo:\n   624→\t\t\tfileinfo, err := os.Stat(path)\n   625→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   626→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get target file info. err: %w, filepath: %s\", err, path)\n   627→\t\t\t}\n   628→\t\t\tf.Filemode = fileinfo.Mode().Perm()\n   629→\t\t\tf.Contents, err = os.ReadFile(path)\n   630→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   631→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to read target file contents. err: %w, filepath: %s\", err, path)\n   632→\t\t\t}\n   633→\t\tdefault:\n   634→\t\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(`stat -c \"%%a\" %s`, path)\n   635→\t\t\tr := exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n   636→\t\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   637→\t\t\t\treturn 640→\t\t\tperm, err := strconv.ParseUint(permStr, 8, 32)\n   641→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   642→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to parse permission string. err: %w, permission string: %s\", err, permStr)\n   643→\t\t\t}\n   644→\t\t\tf.Filemode = os.FileMode(perm)\n   645→\n   646→\t\t\tcmd = fmt.Sprintf(\"cat %s\", path)\n   647→\t\t\tr = exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n   648→\t\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   649→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get target file contents: %s, filepath: %s\", r, path)\n   650→\t\t\t}\n   651→\t\t\tf.Contents = []byte(r.Stdout)\n   652→\t\t}\n   653→\t\tlibFilemap[path] = f\n   654→\t}\n   655→\n   656→\tvar libraryScanners []models.LibraryScanner\n   657→\tif libraryScanners, err = AnalyzeLibraries(context.Background(), libFilemap, l.ServerInfo.Mode.IsOffline()); err != nil {\n   658→\t\treturn err\n   659→\t}\n   660→\tl.LibraryScanners = append(l.LibraryScanners, libraryScanners...)\n   661→\treturn nil\n   662→}\n   663→\n 701→\t\t\tpath,\n   702→\t\t\t&DummyFileInfo{size: int64(len(f.Contents)), filemode: f.Filemode},\n   703→\t\t\tfunc() (dio.ReadSeekCloserAt, error) { return dio.NopCloser(bytes.NewReader(f.Contents)), nil },\n   704→\t\t\tnil,\n   705→\t\t\tanalyzer.AnalysisOptions{Offline: isOffline},\n   706→\t\t); err != nil {\n   707→\t\t\treturn nil, 725→\n   726→// Name is\n   727→func (d *DummyFileInfo) Name() string { return \"dummy\" }\n   728→\n   729→// Size is\n   730→func (d *DummyFileInfo) Size() int64 { return d.size }\n   731→\n detectScanDest() map[string][]string {\n   860→\tscanIPPortsMap := map[string][]string{}\n   861→\n   862→\tfor _, p := range l.osPackages.Packages {\n   863→\t\tif p.AffectedProcs == nil {\n 898→\treturn uniqScanDestIPPorts\n   899→}\n   900→\n   901→func (l *base) execPortsScan(scanDestIPPorts map[string][]string) ([]string, error) {\n   902→\tif 919→\tl.log.Info(\"Using Port Scanner: Vuls built-in Scanner\")\n   920→\n   921→\tlistenIPPorts := []string{}\n   922→\n   923→\tfor ip, ports := range scanDestIPPorts {\n   924→\t\tif !isLocalExec(l.ServerInfo.Port, l.ServerInfo.Host) && net.ParseIP(ip).IsLoopback() {\n   925→\t\t\tcontinue\n   926→\t\t}\n   927→\n   928→\t\tfor _, port := range ports {\n   929→\t\t\tscanDest := ip + \":\" + port\n   930→\t\t\tisOpen, err := nativeScanPort(scanDest)\n   931→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   932→\t\t\t\treturn []string{}, err\n   933→\t\t\t}\n   934→\n   935→\t\t\tif isOpen {\n nativeScanPort(scanDest string) (bool, error) {\n   945→\tconn, err := net.DialTimeout(\"tcp\", scanDest, time.Duration(1)*time.Second)\n   946→\tif err != nil {\n   947→\t\tif strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"i/o timeout\") || strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"connection refused\") {\n   948→\t\t\treturn false, nil\n   949→\t\t}\n   950→\t\tif strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"too many open files\") {\n   951→\t\t\ttime.Sleep(time.Duration(1) * time.Second)\n   952→\t\t\treturn nativeScanPort(scanDest)\n   953→\t\t}\n   954→\t\treturn false, err\n   955→\t}\n   956→\tconn.Close()\n   957→\n   958→\treturn true, nil\n   959→}\n   960→\n   961→func (l *base) execExternalPortScan(scanDestIPPorts map[string][]string) ([]string, error) {\n   962→\tportScanConf := l.getServerInfo().PortScan\n   963→\tl.log.Infof(\"Using Port Scanner: External Scanner(PATH: %s)\", portScanConf.ScannerBinPath)\n   964→\tl.log.Infof(\"External Scanner Apply Options: Scan 992→\t\t\tscanner.AddOptions(nmap.WithUnprivileged())\n   993→\t\t}\n   994→\n   995→\t\tif portScanConf.SourcePort != \"\" {\n   996→\t\t\tport, err := strconv.ParseUint(portScanConf.SourcePort, 10, 1005→\t\t\tscanner.AddOptions(nmap.WithTargets(ip[1:len(ip)-1]), nmap.WithPorts(ports...), nmap.WithIPv6Scanning())\n  1006→\t\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-p\", strings.Join(ports, \",\"), 1010→\t\t}\n  1011→\n  1012→\t\tl.log.Debugf(\"Executing... %s\", strings.Replace(strings.Join(cmd, \" \"), \"\\n\", \"\", -1))\n  1013→\t\tresult, warnings, err := scanner.Run()\n  1014→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1015→\t\t\treturn []string{}, xerrors.Errorf(\"unable to run nmap scan: %w\", err)\n  1016→\t\t}\n  1017→\n  1018→\t\tif warnings != nil {\n  1019→\t\t\tl.log.Warnf(\"nmap scan warnings: %s\", warnings)\n  1020→\t\t}\n  1021→\n  1022→\t\tfor _, host := range result.Hosts {\n  1023→\t\t\tif len(host.Ports) == 0 || len(host.Addresses) == 0 {\n  1024→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1025→\t\t\t}\n  1039→func formatNmapOptionsToString(conf *config.PortScanConf) string {\n  1040→\tcmd := []string{conf.ScannerBinPath}\n  1041→\tif len(conf.ScanTechniques) != 0 {\n  1042→\t\tfor _, technique := 1057→\n  1058→func (l *base) setScanTechniques() (func(*nmap.Scanner), error) {\n  1059→\tscanTechniques := l.getServerInfo().PortScan.GetScanTechniques()\n  1060→\n  1061→\tif len(scanTechniques) == 1068→\tfor _, technique := range scanTechniques {\n  1069→\t\tswitch technique {\n  1070→\t\tcase config.TCPSYN:\n  1071→\t\t\treturn nmap.WithSYNScan(), nil\n  1072→\t\tcase config.TCPConnect:\n  1073→\t\t\treturn nmap.WithConnectScan(), nil\n  1074→\t\tcase config.TCPACK:\n  1075→\t\t\treturn nmap.WithACKScan(), nil\n  1076→\t\tcase config.TCPWindow:\n  1077→\t\t\treturn 1082→\t\tcase config.TCPFIN:\n  1083→\t\t\treturn nmap.WithTCPFINScan(), nil\n  1084→\t\tcase config.TCPXmas:\n  1085→\t\t\treturn nmap.WithTCPXmasScan(), nil\n  1086→\t\t}\n  1087→\t}\n  1088→\n  1089→\treturn nil, xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to setScanTechniques. There is an unsupported option in ScanTechniques.\")\n  1090→}\n  1091→\n  1092→func (l *base) updatePortStatus(listenIPPorts []string) {\n  1093→\tfor name, p := range l.osPackages.Packages {\n  1094→\t\tif p.AffectedProcs == nil {\n  1095→\t\t\tcontinue\n  1096→\t\t}\n  1097→\t\tfor i, proc := range p.AffectedProcs {\n  1098→\t\t\tif proc.ListenPortStats == nil {\n  1099→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n *base) detectRunningOnAws() (ok bool, instanceID string, err error) {\n\tif r := l.exec(\"type curl\", noSudo); r.isSuccess() {\n\t\tcmd := \"curl --max-time 1 --noproxy 169.254.169.254 false, \"\", nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true, id, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch r.ExitStatus {\n\t\tcase 28, 7:\n\t\t\t// Not running on AWS\n\t\t\t//  7   Failed to connect to host.\n\t\t\t// 28  operation timeout.\n\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif r := l.exec(\"type wget\", noSudo); r.isSuccess() {\n\t\tcmd := \"wget --tries=3 --timeout=1 --no-proxy -q -O - http://169.254.169.254/latest/meta-data/instance-id\"\n\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, noSudo)\n\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n\t\t\tid := strings.TrimSpace(r.Stdout)\n\t\t\tif !l.isAwsInstanceID(id) {\n\t\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true, id, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch r.ExitStatus {\n\t\tcase 4, 8:\n\t\t\t// Not running on AWS\n\t\t\t// 4   Network failure\n\t\t\t// 8   Server issued an error response.\n\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false, \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\n\t\t\"Failed to curl or wget to AWS instance metadata on %s. container: %s\",\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.ServerName, l.ServerInfo.Container.Name)\n}\n\n// http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSEC2/latest/UserGuide/resource-ids.html\nvar awsInstanceIDPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`^i-[0-9a-f]+$`)\n\nfunc (l *base) isAwsInstanceID(str string) bool {\n\treturn awsInstanceIDPattern.MatchString(str)\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) convertToModel() models.ScanResult {\n\tctype := l.ServerInfo.ContainerType\n\tif l.ServerInfo.Container.ContainerID != \"\" && ctype == \"\" {\n\t\tctype = \"docker\"\n\t}\n\tcontainer := models.Container{\n\t\tContainerID: https://unix.stackexchange.com/questions/196166/how-to-find-out-if-a-system-uses-sysv-upstart-or-systemd-initsystem\nfunc (l *base) detectInitSystem() (string, error) {\n\tvar f func(string) (string, error)\n\tf = func(cmd string) (string, error) {\n\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, sudo)\n\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to stat %s: %s\", cmd, r)\n\t\t}\n\t\tscanner := strings.Contains(line, \"upstart\") {\n\t\t\treturn upstart, nil\n\t\t} else if strings.Contains(line, \"File: ‘/proc/1/exe’ -> ‘/sbin/init’\") ||\n\t\t\tstrings.Contains(line, \"File: `/proc/1/exe' -> `/sbin/init'\") {\n\t\t\treturn f(\"stat /sbin/init\")\n\t\t} else if line == \"File: ‘/sbin/init’\" ||\n\t\t\tline == \"File: `/sbin/init'\" {\n\t\t\tr := l.exec(\"/sbin/init --version\", noSudo)\n\t\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n\t\t\t\tif strings.Contains(r.Stdout, \"upstart\") {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn upstart, nil\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn sysVinit, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to detect a init system: %s\", line)\n\t}\n\treturn f(\"stat /proc/1/exe\")\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) detectServiceName(pid string) (string, error) {\n\tcmd := content\ntype LibFile struct {\n\tContents []byte\n\tFilemode os.FileMode\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) scanLibraries() (err error) {\n\tif len(l.LibraryScanners) != 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// library scan for servers need lockfiles\n\tif len(l.ServerInfo.Lockfiles) == 0 && !l.ServerInfo.FindLock {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tl.log.Info(\"Scanning Lockfile...\")\n\n\tlibFilemap := {\n\t\t\tfindopt += fmt.Sprintf(\"-name %q -o \", filename)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// delete last \"-o \"\n\t\t// find / -type f -and \\( -name \"package-lock.json\" -o -name \"yarn.lock\" ... \\) 2>&1 | grep strconv.ParseUint(permStr, 8, 32)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to parse permission string. err: %w, permission string: %s\", err, permStr)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tf.Filemode contents: %s, filepath: %s\", r, path)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tf.Contents = []byte(r.Stdout)\n\t\t}\n\t\tlibFilemap[path] = f\n\t}\n\n\tvar libraryScanners []models.LibraryScanner\n\tif libraryScanners, err = []analyzer.Type{\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeAlpine,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeAlma,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeAmazon,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeDebian,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypePhoton,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeCentOS,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeFedora,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeOracle,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeRedHatBase,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeRocky,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeSUSE,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeUbuntu,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeApk,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeDpkg,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeRpm,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeApkCommand,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeYaml,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeTOML,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeJSON,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeDockerfile,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeHCL,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeSecret,\n\t}\n\tanal map[string][]string {\n\tscanIPPortsMap := map[string][]string{}\n\n\tfor _, p := range l.osPackages.Packages {\n\t\tif p.AffectedProcs == nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, proc := range {\n\t\t\t\tm[e] = true\n\t\t\t\tuniqScanDestIPPorts[i] = append(uniqScanDestIPPorts[i], e)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn uniqScanDestIPPorts\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) execPortsScan(scanDestIPPorts []string{}\n\n\tfor ip, ports := range scanDestIPPorts {\n\t\tif !isLocalExec(l.ServerInfo.Port, l.ServerInfo.Host) && net.ParseIP(ip).IsLoopback() {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, port := range = append(listenIPPorts, scanDest)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn listenIPPorts, nil\n}\n\nfunc nativeScanPort(scanDest string) (bool, error) {\n\tconn, err := net.DialTimeout(\"tcp\", scanDest, time.Duration(1)*time.Second)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"i/o timeout\") || strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"connection refused\") {\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tif strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"too many open files\") {\n\t\t\ttime.Sleep(time.Duration(1) * time.Second)\n\t\t\treturn nativeScanPort(scanDest)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn false, err\n\t}\n\tconn.Close()\n\n\treturn true, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) execExternalPortScan(scanDestIPPorts map[string][]string) ([]string, error) {\n\tportScanConf := l.getServerInfo().PortScan\n\tl.log.Infof(\"Using Port Scanner: External Scanner(PATH: %s)\", portScanConf.ScannerBinPath)\n\tl.log.Infof(\"External Scanner Apply Options: Scan Techniques: %s, HasPrivileged: %t, Source Port: %s\",\n\t\tstrings.Join(portScanConf.ScanTechniques, \",\"), portScanConf.HasPrivileged, portScanConf.SourcePort)\n\tbaseCmd := formatNmapOptionsToString(portScanConf)\n\n\tlistenIPPorts := []string{}\n\n\tfor ip, ports := range scanDestIPPorts {\n\t\tif !isLocalExec(l.ServerInfo.Port, l.ServerInfo.Host) && net.ParseIP(ip).IsLoopback() {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t_, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Minute)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tscanner, err :=
